\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{clearTexture()}{clearTexture()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sketch\+::clear\+Texture (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{k }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}



clear texture, k = 0 -\/ background, k = 1 -\/ text, anything else will cause segment fault 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em k} & integer, index of textures, 0 will be background, 1 will be text if tes\mbox{[}k\mbox{]} is nullptr, do nothing call SDL\+\_\+\+Destroy\+Texture and after that set tes\mbox{[}k\mbox{]} to be nullptr \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{Data\_Structures@{Data\_Structures}!initFont@{initFont}}
\index{initFont@{initFont}!Data\_Structures@{Data\_Structures}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{initFont()}{initFont()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sketch\+::init\+Font (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{Button_8hpp_ab701e3ac61a85b337ec5c1abaad6742d}{json}} \&}]{mem }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}



init font from json 

if mem is not contain \char`\"{}font\char`\"{} key, do nothing

get font file and combine with \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceGLOBAL_a490a4d88702b315d3fb722da831114b5}{GLOBAL\+::\+Fonts\+Folder}} to get full path of font file

source font from that path and source the size of the font

if in \char`\"{}font\char`\"{} object contain \char`\"{}rect\char`\"{} key, get rect text

if in \char`\"{}font\char`\"{} object contain \char`\"{}color\char`\"{} key, get color text

if int \char`\"{}font\char`\"{} object contain \char`\"{}text\char`\"{}, set default text of sketch to be mem\mbox{[}\char`\"{}font\char`\"{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\char`\"{}text\char`\"{}\mbox{]}

example of param mem\+:

\{

\char`\"{}font\char`\"{}\+: \{ \begin{DoxyVerb} "name": "font.ttf",

 "size": 0,

 "rect": {

      "x": 0,

      "y": 0,

      "w": 0,

      "h": 0

},

"color": {

      "r": 0,

      "g": 0,

      "b": 0,

      "a": 0

},

"text": "text"
\end{DoxyVerb}
 \}

\}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mem} & json, contain font of sketch \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
